margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">Indicate by check mark whether the Registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this chapter) or Rule <span style="white-space:nowrap">12b-2</span> of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#167;240.12b-2</span> of this chapter).</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:right">Emerging growth company&#160;&#160;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" contextRef="duration_2020-12-29_to_2020-12-29" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></span></p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the Registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section&#160;13(a) of the Exchange Act.&#160;&#160;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9744;</span></p> <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p></div></div> <p style='page-break-before:always'></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" /> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">

<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;5.02</span></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers.</p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">On December&#160;29, 2020, the Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of Apple Inc. appointed Ms.&#160;Monica Lozano to Apple&#8217;s Board, effective as of January&#160;4, 2021. Ms.&#160;Lozano will serve on the Audit and Finance Committee of the Board.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">As a <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-employee</span> director, Ms.&#160;Lozano will receive a $100,000 annual retainer for her service on the Board, paid in quarterly installments, and participate in the Apple Inc. <span style="white-space:nowrap">Non-Employee</span> Director Stock Plan, as amended and restated as of February&#160;13, 2018 (the <span style="white-space:nowrap">&#8220;Non-Employee</span> Director Plan&#8221;), which was filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;SEC&#8221;) on February&#160;14, 2018 as Exhibit 10.1 to Apple&#8217;s Current Report on <span style="white-space:nowrap">Form&#160;8-K.</span> On the effective day of her appointment, Ms.&#160;Lozano received an automatic initial grant of 281 restricted stock units under the <span style="white-space:nowrap">Non-Employee</span> Director Plan. In connection with her appointment, Apple and Ms.&#160;Lozano will enter into Apple&#8217;s standard indemnification agreement for directors, the form of which was filed with the SEC on July&#160;22,&#160;2009 as Exhibit 10.2 to Apple&#8217;s Quarterly Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</span> for the quarterly period ended June&#160;27, 2009.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">There are no transactions between Apple and Ms.&#160;Lozano that would be required to be reported under Item&#160;404(a) of Regulation <span style="white-space:nowrap">S-K.</span></p></div></div> <p style='page-break-before:always'></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" /> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto"> <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold;text-align:center">SIGNATURES</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;text-align:justify">Pursuant to the requirements of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, the Registrant has duly caused this report to be signed on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
